Through this resolution, we convey our determination and attitude towards upholding human rights.â€  Ms. Tang said that currently there is a poster exhibition about the organ harvesting in Kaohsiung Girls Senior High. She said everyone needs to uphold human rights.   Kaohsiung City Councilor Cai Jinyan  Kaohsiung City Councilor Cai Jinyan said, â€œLive organ harvesting is a severe oppression of life.
